+// === GET DYNAMIC SURVEY QUESTIONS ===
+app.get('/surveys', async (req, res) => {
+  try {
+    const result = await pool.query(
+      'SELECT id, question_text, target_level, target_category, tedil_code FROM surveys ORDER BY id ASC'
+    );
+    res.json({ success: true, questions: result.rows });
+  } catch (err) {
+    console.error('Error (GET /surveys):', err);
+    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Server error while fetching survey.' });
+  }
+});
